let me start by saying , let's look back to the 20th century , and kind of get a sense of how that style of security worked for us .	讓我先來回顧一下二十世紀 , 有點像是了解安全風格對我們來說是如何運作的 。
this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the nato headquarters in belgium .	這是verdun , 一個法國的戰場 , 就在北約在比利時總部的北邊 。
at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	1916年 , 在verdun這個地方 , 超過300天 , 70萬人被殺 , 所以大約每天有2000人被殺 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	如果再向前推進二十世紀的安全 , 進入第二次世界大戰 , 你看到史達林格的戰爭 , 300天 , 兩百萬人被殺 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們進入冷戰 , 繼續建造圍牆 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從一戰的壕溝 , 到第二次世界大戰的馬其頓戰線 , 再到冷戰中的鐵幕 , 柏林牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天的主題是 , 我們不再建牆 , 而是建設安全 , 我們要建造橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲一座著名的橋 。
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	它是drina河的橋樑 , 由ivoandric所設計的小說的主題 , 它談到如何在歐洲和巴爾幹地區非常麻煩的部分 , 經過一段時間又建了巨大的牆 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	更近期 , 在過去十年 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 猶豫著要團結在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我想再次重申 , 開放式安全是關乎國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人的和公共的 , 並與策略性的溝通交流 , 主要在社交網路上 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為我們的全球公有物會受到各種方式的攻擊 , 且對全球公有物的源頭都不會被通過築牆來解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	現在 , 我是一個水手 , 顯然
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一艘線船 , 在印度洋上航行 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張圖有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	它的側邊有協奏曲線 ,
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	也就是防止海盜來襲擊
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	海盜是現今全世界都很活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	海盜在馬拉卡的海峽也很活躍
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	活躍在幾內亞灣 ,
we see it in the caribbean .	我們看到在加勒比海
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	在全球交通運輸系統中 , 每一百億美金的損失 ,
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 在這個時期 , 有20艘船 , 500名船員被挾持人質 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是對全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要考慮如何解決
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉到另一種海洋 , 像是網路之海 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這裡有兩個年輕人的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	在當下 , 他們被監禁著 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們進行了一個信用卡詐騙案 , 網另外還不到100億美元 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分網路犯罪是全球經濟2兆美元的不連續性
two trillion a year .	每年兩兆 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	那只是在英國的國內生產總值之下
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以這個無止境的網路海 , 我們知道它是激進開放的基本元素 , 也受到很大的威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	我擔心的另一件事是全球公有物的威脅 , 是被販賣、麻醉劑、鴉片這些毒品的威脅 , 從阿富汗穿過歐洲到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心從andeanridge北部運過來的可卡因 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的運輸 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的可怕代價 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	運輸主要是在海洋中移動 , 但在全球公有物的其他部分 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望能告訴你們 , 這是非常高科技的美國海軍設備 , 我們用它來阻止人口販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是一個販毒集團的半潛水器 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	建在南美洲叢林中的
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用低科技的木筏逮到它 , 它帶著六噸的可卡因 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個隊員 , 精良的溝通都掃了起來
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣 , 在毒品領域 , 在人力 , 武器裡面 , 上帝禁止 , 在大規模毀滅性武器中 , 是造成全球公有物威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	並且讓我們今天一起在阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是在阿富汗的一個熱鬧區 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世上80%到90%的鉀和海洛因來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	當然 , 我們也看到了恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是基地組織建立的地方 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到了一場強烈的暴動發生在那兒 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的擔憂 , 也是全球公有物的一部分 , 也是我們必須要處理的 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以 , 在21世紀 ,
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們20世紀的工具是行不通的 。
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我認為 , 我們不會僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全感 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不能僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們會需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這麼做時 , 我們必須要做得很好 , 且要有能力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關于國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人和公共的聯系 , 通過互聯網溝通而聯繫在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子 , 讓你們知道這是如何運作的 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗的士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說 , " 這太奇怪了 , 我以為我讀到過這個人口統計 , 年輕人和女人在20、30多歲在阿富汗都是不識字的 。 "
you would be correct .	你會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	85%不識字 , 當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 ,
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為在這些男人和女人學會閱讀的期間 , 塔利班的教育就沒有意義 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以 , 問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在北約與私營機構合作時 , 教導他們閱讀讀讀讀讀讀書籍 , 與發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教了超過20萬的阿富汗安全部隊士兵去讀和寫 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你能在阿富汗讀和寫時 , 通常會放一支筆在口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在畢業典禮上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 她們帶著驕傲的筆 , 放進他們的口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	國際事務有五十個國家在這些發展機構和私人和公共事業中涉及的安全 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也教他們格鬥技巧 , 但我要說 , 開放式安全意味著一種能創造更持久安全效應的方式 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	叫做舒適感 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘姊妹船叫做mercy號
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這一個 , 舒適 , 在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在一般的巡迴演出 , 他們會進行40萬個治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	這部電影的船員不是嚴格的被軍事行動 , 而是結合人道組織:運營希望、計劃微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織送來志願者
interagency physicians come out .	各國的醫師會出面
they're all part of this .	他們都是這其中的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他的媽媽走了兩天來到安慰號上的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被適應時 , 用他極端的微弱眼睛 , 他突然抬頭 , 說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽媽 , 我看到世界了 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	把這個數字乘以40萬的治療方式 , 這個私人和公共的合作是有保安力量的 , 你開始發現創造安全的力量是非常不同的 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到棒球選手
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在這張照片裡挑出兩名美軍士兵嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這群小男孩兩邊的小伙子 。 這是一系列棒球診所的其中一員 , 我們在國際聯盟棒球比賽中探討合作 , 設立了各個部門 , 軍隊棒球選手 , 他們是真正的軍人 , 但他們參與了這項使命 , 他們把診所開到了拉丁美洲和加勒比地區 , 開到了宏都拉斯 , 開到了整個美洲和加拉瓜 , 開到了整個中美洲 , 開到了加拉瓜 , 開到了全美洲 , 開到了加拉尼亞和加拉瓜 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕男女展現榜樣 , 關於體良以及生命的重要性 , 我主張是要幫我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這種合作的另一面在災難救援中
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍的直升機 , 參與2004年海嘯後 , 造成25萬人死亡 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些重大災難中2004年的海嘯 , 25萬人死亡 , 2005年巴基斯坦的喀什米爾地震 , 8萬5千人死亡 , 海地震 , 30萬人死亡 , 最近發生了可怕的地震災害 , 襲擊日本核工業 , 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際間的合作夥伴 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共部門合作 , 合作用這種自然災害 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些是關於開放式安全的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它綁在一起 , 逐漸地 , 做成這樣的事情 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看到的這個是想 " 啊 , 沒道理 , 這些一定是通信交流的海道 , 或者這些是光纖電纜 。 "
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 ! 這張圖是根據twitter所畫的
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 。 綠色是地點 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成的 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是很棒的人口調查中 , 六大國家依次排名世界 。 中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特 , 和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	我們為什麼要買這些漁網呢 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	為什麼我們想要參與其中 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們之前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦發表一個像這樣的演講 , 講到這個 。 我對你們說 , 我在facebook上 , 請親愛的 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	聽眾的笑聲 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	曾經有一篇ap的文章 , 由ap所主導 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	被帶到世界上兩個地方:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北約艾德米爾需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是一名催化劑第二天早上我就有上百個facebook好友請求 , 來自印尼和芬蘭多半的請求 , 大多是說: 「 記者 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 哦 , 對了 , nato是甚麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是啊 , 我們笑了 , 但這是我們如何移動這個訊息 , 移動那個訊息就是我們如何連結國際間 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共 , 還有這些社群網絡 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 我來談談一個嚴肅的事實 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這張照片是一位勇敢的英國士兵 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他正在helmand站崗 , 在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡來提醒我們 , 我不希望有人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要能夠創造真正的軍事力量 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	那就是我們是誰以及我們做什麼的核心我們為了保護自由 , 言論自由和所有我們在社會中珍視的事物
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但是 , 你知道 , 生命不是一個開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有一支軍隊 , 不是在戰鬥中 , 就是在兵營中 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會說 , 人生是個混亂者 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須調一個數值 , 並且就像我思考我們在21世紀中如何創造安全一樣 , 有時候我們在真正的戰爭和危機中運用硬實力 , 但是會有很多的例子 , 就像我們今天說的 , 我們的軍隊可以成為創造21世紀安全的一部分 , 國際 , 跨部門 , 公私結合的 , 與能力溝通聯繫在一起的一部分 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	我最後想說的是 , 今天早些時候聽到的關于維基百科 。 我經常使用維基百科查事實 , 正如你們所有人所欣賞的 , 維基百科不是靠12個聰明的人把自己關在房間裡寫文章創造出來的 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科每天有數萬人輸入資料每天都有數百萬人關注這些資訊
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	它是一個完美的圖像 , 可以說明我們當中沒有一個人是那麼聰明的 , 和我們所有人一起思考一樣 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有一個人像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的宣言很簡單:一個每個人可以自由地在所有知識的總和之下分享 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 藉由結合國際 , 跨部門 , 公私的 , 戰略通信 , 共同在21世紀 , 我們就能創造出安全的總和 。
